 Bhaiyaram Yadav's parents, who live in Bharatpur village in Karvi tehsil of Chitrakoot, had taught them to befriend trees since childhood
 bhaiyaram ko apane mata-pita se mili yah sikh us samay junun main badal gai, jab uske bete or patni kaa dehanth ho gaya

 "the Ministry of Labor has issued a statement clarifying that the proposed amendment will not make the payment of salary mandatory only through check or account
 bayaan main kaha gaya ki upyukt sarkaar (centre yaa rajya) khaas udyogon yaa anya pratishthanon ke liye adhisuchana jari karengi jahaan niyokta ko kamgaaron ko vetan kaa bhugtan check yaa karmchaariyon ke khaaton main paise sthaanantarit kar karnaa hoga

 " The statement said, "employers can no longer show a reduced number of employees to avoid becoming a contributor to an employee provident fund organization or employee state insurance corporation plan
 " The ministry also informed that states like Andhra Pradesh, Telangana, Kerala, Uttarakhand, Punjab and Haryana have already issued notification for payment of wages through banking channels

 isliye, lekha pareekshakon ko audit puraa karne or apni report pesh karne kii koshish kerani chahie

 lekin company adhinium 2013 ne use badal diya

 According to the law, an auditor, during an audit, has a good reason to believe that the officers or employees of the company have committed fraud of Rs one crore or more, then he must immediately report the suspected fraud to the company's audit committee
 needed

 loksabhaa main purvahn 11 baje kaarywahi shuru hote hi bhartiya janata party (bhaajapa), marxvaadi communist party (makapa) tathaa trinmul congress ke sadasyon ne narebaaji shuru kar di

 dopaher main kaarywahi shuru hone par bhi yahi sthiti jari rahi, jis kaaran unhone sadan kii kaarywahi dopaher do baje tak ke liye sthagit kar di

 Palestinian Prime Minister Rami Hamdalla was killed during a visit to the Gaza Strip
 yah jaankaree philistin ke grih mantralay ne di he
 According to the information of the Home Ministry, on Tuesday, when the Prime Minister and his convoy were traveling to the Gaza Strip, the convoy was targeted and attacked
 is jaanaleva hamale main philistini pradhanmantri bal-bal bache
 According to the news agency report, Hamdalla had come to Gaza to inaugurate a wastewater treatment plant and meet officials
 usee dauraan unpar hamalaa kiya gaya
 While the Palestinian news agency Wafa said Hamdalla and Majid Faraj, the head of the Palestinian Intelligence Service, narrowly survived the blast
 is visphot main kul saat log ghayal hue he
 The Palestinian National Authority blamed Hamas for the explosion
 bataa den ki abhi tak kisi bhi sanghathan ne visphot kii jimmedaari nahin lee he
 According to the newspapers in Kerala, there are about 36,000 small and big temples in the state i
e
 around 3
 5 karod kii aabaadi main lagbhag 1,000 logon par ek mandir
 If other religious sites are added, then on average 900 people account for one religious center
 bharat main dharmik sthalon kii gananaa kaa koi thos aankada uplabdh nahin he lekin kerala ko sample maanakar yah andaja lagaaya ja saktaa he ki aabaadi or dharmik sthalon kaa lagbhag yahi ausat kamobesh puure desh main hoga
 This average is much larger than any public service in hospitals, schools, police stations, railway stations, etc
 per one thousand people in India
 aarthik gananaaon main dharm kaa community sarvice ke taur par moolyankan nahin hota lekin buniyadi dhaanche, vyavasthaaon, vistaar, jan bhagidaari main dharmik tantra bharat kii sabase badi saamudayik seva he, jiskaa apana paryaapt sakasham or bada arthshaastra bhi he
 We should regret that our greatest community service, vast, prosperous and deeply intertwined with politics, cannot guarantee the human rights that people will not lose their lives by cherishing beliefs
 kollam kii jali-bhuni jindagiyon ke liye aatishbaajee kii pratispardhaa ko jimmedaar maananaa galati hogi, thik usee tarah jaise ki hamane aktubar 2013 main datia (madhya pradesh) ke ratangarh mandir main 121 maut vaali bhagdad ke sabak, mandir ke paas bane kamjor pul main talashne kii koshish kii thi
 The geography of these places was not responsible for 36 deaths in a stampede at Allahabad station during Kumbh in 2013 or 249 deaths in Chamunda Devi (mehrangarh in Rajasthan) in 2008
 jimmedaar to ham hai jo aasthaa se jude is vishaal tantra ko gambhirtha se nahin lete
 Hone hum tech surma but crowd management at most religious places is actually like sheep management
 bana rakhe honge hamane bhawan nirmaan ke darjanon kaayade-kanoon lekin sarkaar kaa vishaal tantra dharmik sthal main nunatam buniyadi dhaancha sunishchit nahin kar paata
 Our religion managers can fight up to the largest court to prevent women from entering temples but will not give ear to the court order (supreme Court 2013) to secure people's lives in temples
 hamaara dharmik-rajnatik netritv sookhe ko lekar ek sant ke betuke bayaan par ghanton bahes kar saktaa he lekin dharmik sthalon ko surakshit banane kii jimmedaari tay karne ke liye koi bahes nahin hogi
 Religion as a community service sets India apart from the world
 sarkaar to yah nahin bataa sakati ki dharmik sthalon kii kul sankhya kitni he lekin agar ham kuch nijee adhyayanon, dharmik vishleshanon or dharm sanghathanon kaa aankada khangaalen to hamen is saamudayik seva ke vistaar kaa aayam chaunkaa degaa
 There are around 5,000 Hindu mythological pilgrimages active in India, references to which come from ancient literature or history
 buddha, jain, islam, sikh, isai kendron ko milakar yah sankhya 6,000 se upar nikal jaati he
 There are about 60 big religious cities in India where the whole city revolves around a religious center
 yakeenan is gananaa main dharm sthalon kaa vishaal sthaneey tantra shaamil nahin he jo shaharon va gramin basaavaton ke bich sabase teji se failane vaala network he
 Pilgrimage and religious tourism, seasonal fairs, worship and festivities are also part of this vast network which, after incorporating, only on the basis of people's participation, religion becomes a community service that is more chalky than any other community service
 Asks for arrangement kya ham khud se yah poochne kaa saahas juta sakate hai ki koi desh apni itani badi seva ko is tarah chalaaegaa jaise ki bharat main dharmik sthal chalate hai
 Religious centers in India's socio-economic structure are tangible assets that mobilize resources, employ people and grow their activities to become large economies in order to remain in the social environment
 saamaajik-aarthik sampatti ke aadhaar par bharat kii yah saamudayik seva teen tarah kii asangatiyon kii shikaar he
 The first of these is the lack of capacities - this system, which serves the largest part of India's population on a daily, weekly, monthly and yearly basis, does not have the capabilities as per demand
 dharmik tirthon ke network se lekar majhole mandiron tak, kshamta kii yah kami hameshaa najar aati he jo bheed prabandhan or suraksha tak kii chunautiyon ke taur par saamne aati he
 The second inconsistency is lack of regulation
 dharmik sthalon ko banane yaa chalaane ke koi niyam nahin hai
 Being a religious center, most of the sites are beyond all kinds of construction rules, in which there is no system for cleanliness, pollution and public amenities

 The camp that was ravaged was not a normal launch pad or base
 nasht kiye gaye aatanki camp main firing range, visphotak pareekshan suvidhaayen, prashikshakon ke liye vaataanukoolit karyaalay, prashikshan le rahe aatankiyon ke liye vahaan par barrack bhi the
